The two children kept shouting that it was hot, so I called the front desk to ask. He told me that the air conditioner was short-circuited and broken because the children were already taking a shower in it. I thought I'd just make do with it. They gave us a small fan, but it was still very hot. I slept all night because it was hot and I didn't sleep well. I felt stuffy and lacked oxygen.
